[2024-10-28 20:29:03] Generated objective: Implement a snippet that constructs a complete early-game power and automation setup by placing and connecting an offshore pump, boiler, and steam engine array, then establishes coal mining with inserters feeding both the boiler and an adjacent assembling machine production line, ensuring proper electric pole coverage and pipe connections throughout the system.
[2024-10-28 20:29:15] # Find water and setup initial power
water_loc = nearest(Resource.Water)
move_to(water_loc)

# Place and connect power generation
pump = place_entity(Prototype.OffshorePump, position=water_loc)
pump_dir = Direction(pump.direction)
opposite_dir = Direction.opposite(pump_dir)

boiler = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.Boiler,
                             reference_position=pump.position,
                             direction=opposite_dir,
                             spacing=2)
boiler = rotate_entity(boiler, Direction.next_clockwise(pump_dir))

water_pipes = connect_entities(pump, boiler, connection_type=Prototype.Pipe)
assert water_pipes

engine = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.SteamEngine,
                             reference_position=boiler.position,
                             direction=boiler.direction,
                             spacing=2)
steam_pipes = connect_entities(boiler, engine, connection_type=Prototype.Pipe)
assert steam_pipes

# Setup coal mining and transport
coal_inserter = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter,
                                    reference_position=boiler.position,
                                    direction=Direction.RIGHT,
                                    spacing=1)
coal_inserter = rotate_entity(coal_inserter, Direction.LEFT)

move_to(nearest(Resource.Coal))
drill = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, position=nearest(Resource.Coal))
drill_inserter = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter,
                                     reference_position=drill.position,
                                     direction=Direction.DOWN,
                                     spacing=1)
drill_inserter = rotate_entity(drill_inserter, Direction.UP)

# Connect mining to boiler with belts
mining_belts = connect_entities(drill, drill_inserter, connection_type=Prototype.TransportBelt)
boiler_belts = connect_entities(mining_belts[0].belts[-1], coal_inserter, connection_type=Prototype.TransportBelt)
assert mining_belts and boiler_belts

# Setup assembler with power
assembler = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.AssemblingMachine1,
                                reference_position=engine.position,
                                direction=Direction.LEFT,
                                spacing=3)

poles = connect_entities(engine, assembler, connection_type=Prototype.SmallElectricPole)
assert poles

# Initialize mining
drill = insert_item(Prototype.Coal, drill, 5)

# Verify setup
sleep(10)
assembler_status = inspect_entities(assembler.position, radius=1).get_entity(Prototype.AssemblingMachine1)
assert not assembler_status.warning

                     direction=Direction.RIGHT, 
                     position=Position(x=boiler.position.x + 6, y=boiler.position.y))

                           direction=Direction.LEFT,
                           position=Position(x=boiler.position.x, y=boiler.position.y + 1))

boiler_belts = connect_entities(mining_belts[-1], coal_inserter, connection_type=Prototype.TransportBelt)

drill_inserter = insert_item(Prototype.Coal, drill_inserter, 1)

iron_patch = get_resource_patch(Resource.IronOre, nearest(Resource.IronOre))
assert coal_patch and iron_patch, "Required resource patches not found"

# Set up coal mining

move_to(coal_drill_pos)

# Place coal collection belt

assert coal_belt, "Failed to place coal collection belt"

water_location = nearest(Resource.Water)
move_to(water_location)

# Place and setup offshore pump
offshore_pump = place_entity(Prototype.OffshorePump, position=water_location)
pump_connection = offshore_pump.connection_points[0]

# Place and setup boiler
boiler = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.Boiler,
                             reference_position=offshore_pump.position, 
                             direction=Direction.RIGHT,
                             spacing=1)

# Connect pump to boiler with pipes
connect_entities(offshore_pump, boiler, connection_type=Prototype.Pipe)

# Place steam engine after boiler
steam_engine = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.SteamEngine,
                                   reference_position=boiler.position,
                                   direction=Direction.RIGHT,
                                   spacing=1)

# Connect boiler to steam engine with pipes

# Add power pole near steam engine

                                 reference_position=steam_engine.position,
                                 direction=Direction.UP,
                                 spacing=1)

# Setup coal mining

burner_drill = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, position=nearest(Resource.Coal))
inserter = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter,
                               reference_position=burner_drill.position,
                               direction=Direction.DOWN,
                               spacing=1)
rotate_entity(inserter, Direction.UP)

# Connect drill to boiler with belts
belts = connect_entities(burner_drill, boiler, connection_type=Prototype.TransportBelt)

# Add initial coal to start system
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, burner_drill, 5)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, inserter, 1) 
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, boiler, 5)

# Wait for power generation
sleep(10)

[2024-10-28 20:32:51] # Find and move to water
water_location = nearest(Resource.Water)
move_to(water_location)

# Place and setup offshore pump facing right
offshore_pump = place_entity(Prototype.OffshorePump, direction=Direction.RIGHT, position=water_location)

# Place and setup boiler with spacing 
boiler = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.Boiler, 
                             reference_position=offshore_pump.position,
                             direction=Direction.RIGHT,
                             spacing=1)

# Connect pump to boiler with pipes
connect_entities(offshore_pump, boiler, connection_type=Prototype.Pipe)

# Place steam engine after boiler with spacing
steam_engine = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.SteamEngine,
                                   reference_position=boiler.position, 
                                   direction=Direction.RIGHT,
                                   spacing=1)

# Connect boiler to steam engine with pipes  
connect_entities(boiler, steam_engine, connection_type=Prototype.Pipe)

# Add power pole near steam engine
power_pole = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.SmallElectricPole,
                                 reference_position=steam_engine.position,
                                 direction=Direction.UP,
                                 spacing=1)

# Setup coal mining
coal_pos = nearest(Resource.Coal)
move_to(coal_pos)

burner_drill = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, direction=Direction.RIGHT, position=coal_pos)

# Place inserter right of drill
inserter = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter,
                               reference_position=burner_drill.position,
                               direction=Direction.RIGHT,
                               spacing=0)

# Connect drill to inserter with belt
connect_entities(burner_drill, inserter, connection_type=Prototype.TransportBelt)

engine1 = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.SteamEngine, boiler1.position, Direction.UP, spacing=1)

# Connect water system
connect_entities(pump, boiler1, Prototype.Pipe)
connect_entities(boiler1, engine1, Prototype.Pipe)

# Place second boiler/engine pair
boiler2 = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.Boiler, boiler1.position, Direction.RIGHT, spacing=2)
rotate_entity(boiler2, Direction.RIGHT)
engine2 = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.SteamEngine, boiler2.position, Direction.UP, spacing=1)
connect_entities(pump, boiler2, Prototype.Pipe)
connect_entities(boiler2, engine2, Prototype.Pipe)

# Set up coal mining
move_to(coal_position)
drill = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, coal_position, Direction.UP)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, drill, 5)

# Transport system to boilers
belt1 = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.TransportBelt, drill.position, Direction.DOWN, spacing=1)
rotate_entity(belt1, Direction.DOWN)

inserter1 = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter, boiler1.position, Direction.DOWN, spacing=1)
rotate_entity(inserter1, Direction.DOWN)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, inserter1, 1)

inserter2 = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter, boiler2.position, Direction.DOWN, spacing=1)
rotate_entity(inserter2, Direction.DOWN)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, inserter2, 1)

# Initial fuel for boilers
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, boiler1, 5)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, boiler2, 5)

# Verify setup
sleep(30)

# Check power generation
engines = inspect_entities(engine1.position, radius=10).get_entities(Prototype.SteamEngine)
for engine in engines:
    assert engine.power_output > 0, "Steam engine not generating power"
    
# Check fuel distribution
boilers = inspect_entities(boiler1.position, radius=10).get_entities(Prototype.Boiler)
for boiler in boilers:
    assert boiler.temperature > 100, "Boiler not receiving enough fuel"
    fuel = inspect_inventory(boiler).get(Prototype.Coal, 0)
    assert fuel > 0, "Boiler running out of fuel"

print("Power plant setup validated and operational")

[2024-10-28 20:35:48] # Find nearest coal patch and water
coal_position = nearest(Resource.Coal)
water_position = nearest(Resource.Water)
assert coal_position and water_position, "Required resources not found"

# Place offshore pump and initial boiler/steam engine setup
move_to(water_position)
pump = place_entity(Prototype.OffshorePump, Direction.UP, water_position)
boiler1 = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.Boiler, pump.position, Direction.UP, spacing=1)
rotate_entity(boiler1, Direction.RIGHT)
engine1 = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.SteamEngine, boiler1.position, Direction.UP, spacing=1)

# Connect water system
connect_entities(pump, boiler1, Prototype.Pipe)
connect_entities(boiler1, engine1, Prototype.Pipe)

# Place second boiler/engine pair
boiler2 = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.Boiler, boiler1.position, Direction.RIGHT, spacing=2)
rotate_entity(boiler2, Direction.RIGHT)
engine2 = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.SteamEngine, boiler2.position, Direction.UP, spacing=1)
connect_entities(pump, boiler2, Prototype.Pipe)
connect_entities(boiler2, engine2, Prototype.Pipe)

# Set up coal mining
move_to(coal_position)
drill = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, Direction.UP, coal_position)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, drill, 5)

# Transport system to boilers
belt1 = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.TransportBelt, drill.position, Direction.DOWN, spacing=1)
rotate_entity(belt1, Direction.DOWN)

inserter1 = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter, boiler1.position, Direction.DOWN, spacing=1)
rotate_entity(inserter1, Direction.DOWN)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, inserter1, 1)

inserter2 = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter, boiler2.position, Direction.DOWN, spacing=1)
rotate_entity(inserter2, Direction.DOWN)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, inserter2, 1)

# Initial fuel for boilers
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, boiler1, 5)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, boiler2, 5)

# Verify setup
sleep(30)

# Check power generation
engines = inspect_entities(engine1.position, radius=10).get_entities(Prototype.SteamEngine)
for engine in engines:
    assert engine.status == EntityStatus.WORKING, "Steam engine not generating power"
    
# Check fuel distribution
boilers = inspect_entities(boiler1.position, radius=10).get_entities(Prototype.Boiler)
for boiler in boilers:
    assert boiler.status == EntityStatus.WORKING, "Boiler not receiving enough fuel"
    fuel = inspect_inventory(boiler).get(Prototype.Coal, 0)
    assert fuel > 0, "Boiler running out of fuel"

print("Power plant setup validated and operational")

# Place offshore pump and initial boiler/steam engine setup
move_to(water_position)
pump = place_entity(Prototype.OffshorePump, Direction.RIGHT, water_position)

# Place first boiler-engine pair
boiler1 = place_entity(Prototype.Boiler, Direction.RIGHT, Position(x=pump.position.x + 3, y=pump.position.y))
engine1 = place_entity(Prototype.SteamEngine, Direction.RIGHT, Position(x=boiler1.position.x + 3, y=boiler1.position.y))

# Place second boiler-engine pair
boiler2 = place_entity(Prototype.Boiler, Direction.RIGHT, Position(x=pump.position.x + 3, y=pump.position.y + 6))
engine2 = place_entity(Prototype.SteamEngine, Direction.RIGHT, Position(x=boiler2.position.x + 3, y=boiler2.position.y))

# Connect water system
pipes1 = connect_entities(pump, boiler1, Prototype.Pipe)
pipes2 = connect_entities(pump, boiler2, Prototype.Pipe)
connect_entities(boiler1, engine1, Prototype.Pipe)
connect_entities(boiler2, engine2, Prototype.Pipe)

# Set up coal mining
move_to(coal_position)
drill = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, Direction.RIGHT, coal_position)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, drill, 5)

# Transport system from miner to boilers
belt_to_boiler1 = connect_entities(drill, Position(x=boiler1.position.x - 1, y=boiler1.position.y), Prototype.TransportBelt)
belt_to_boiler2 = connect_entities(Position(x=boiler1.position.x - 1, y=boiler1.position.y), 
                                 Position(x=boiler2.position.x - 1, y=boiler2.position.y), 
                                 Prototype.TransportBelt)

# Add inserters for boilers
inserter1 = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerInserter, Direction.LEFT, Position(x=boiler1.position.x - 1, y=boiler1.position.y))
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, inserter1, 1)

inserter2 = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerInserter, Direction.LEFT, Position(x=boiler2.position.x - 1, y=boiler2.position.y))
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, inserter2, 1)

# Initial fuel for boilers
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, boiler1, 5)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, boiler2, 5)

# Monitor system operation
for _ in range(4):
    sleep(30)
    
    # Check power generation
    engines = inspect_entities(engine1.position, radius=20).get_entities(Prototype.SteamEngine)
    for engine in engines:
        assert engine.status == EntityStatus.WORKING, "Steam engine not generating power"
        
    # Check fuel distribution  
    boilers = inspect_entities(boiler1.position, radius=20).get_entities(Prototype.Boiler)
    for boiler in boilers:
        assert boiler.status == EntityStatus.WORKING, "Boiler not receiving enough fuel"
        fuel = inspect_inventory(boiler).get(Prototype.Coal, 0)
        assert fuel > 0, "Boiler running out of fuel"

print("Power plant setup validated and operational")

    Position(x=boiler1.position.x - 1, y=boiler1.position.y),

    Prototype.TransportBelt
)

    # Check fuel distribution

    for boiler in boilers:

        fuel = inspect_inventory(boiler).get(Prototype.Coal, 0)
        assert fuel > 0, "Boiler running out of fuel"

    Position(x=boiler1.position.x - 1, y=boiler1.position.y),
    Prototype.TransportBelt
)

    Position(x=boiler2.position.x - 1, y=boiler2.position.y),
    Prototype.TransportBelt
)

    belt = place_entity(Prototype.TransportBelt, Direction.DOWN, current_pos)
    belt_segments.append(belt)
    current_pos = next_pos

# Create belt split to boilers
move_to(current_pos)
split_belt = place_entity(Prototype.TransportBelt, Direction.LEFT, current_pos)

# Connect to boiler 1
current_pos = split_belt.position
while current_pos.x > boiler1.position.x - 1:
    next_pos = Position(x=current_pos.x - 1, y=boiler1.position.y)
    move_to(current_pos)
    belt = place_entity(Prototype.TransportBelt, Direction.LEFT, current_pos)
    current_pos = next_pos

# Connect to boiler 2
current_pos = split_belt.position
while current_pos.x > boiler2.position.x - 1:
    next_pos = Position(x=current_pos.x - 1, y=boiler2.position.y)
    move_to(current_pos)
    belt = place_entity(Prototype.TransportBelt, Direction.LEFT, current_pos)
    current_pos = next_pos

# Add inserters for boilers
inserter1_pos = Position(x=boiler1.position.x - 1, y=boiler1.position.y)
move_to(inserter1_pos)
inserter1 = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerInserter, Direction.LEFT, inserter1_pos)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, inserter1, 1)

inserter2_pos = Position(x=boiler2.position.x - 1, y=boiler2.position.y)
move_to(inserter2_pos)
inserter2 = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerInserter, Direction.LEFT, inserter2_pos)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, inserter2, 1)

# Initial fuel for boilers
move_to(boiler1.position)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, boiler1, 5)
move_to(boiler2.position)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, boiler2, 5)

# Monitor system operation
for _ in range(4):
    sleep(30)
    
    # Check power generation
    engines = inspect_entities(engine1.position, radius=20).get_entities(Prototype.SteamEngine)
    for engine in engines:
        assert engine.status == EntityStatus.WORKING, "Steam engine not generating power"
        
    # Check fuel distribution
    boilers = inspect_entities(boiler1.position, radius=20).get_entities(Prototype.Boiler)
    for boiler in boilers:
        assert boiler.status == EntityStatus.WORKING, "Boiler not receiving enough fuel"
        fuel = inspect_inventory(boiler).get(Prototype.Coal, 0)
        assert fuel > 0, "Boiler running out of fuel"

print("Power plant setup validated and operational")

water_position = nearest(Resource.Water)
assert coal_position and water_position, "Required resources not found"

# Place offshore pump and initial boiler/steam engine setup
move_to(water_position)
pump = place_entity(Prototype.OffshorePump, Direction.RIGHT, water_position)

# Place first boiler-engine pair
boiler1_pos = Position(x=pump.position.x + 3, y=pump.position.y) 
move_to(boiler1_pos)
boiler1 = place_entity(Prototype.Boiler, Direction.RIGHT, boiler1_pos)
engine1_pos = Position(x=boiler1.position.x + 3, y=boiler1.position.y)
move_to(engine1_pos)
engine1 = place_entity(Prototype.SteamEngine, Direction.RIGHT, engine1_pos)

# Place second boiler-engine pair
boiler2_pos = Position(x=pump.position.x + 3, y=pump.position.y + 3)
move_to(boiler2_pos)
boiler2 = place_entity(Prototype.Boiler, Direction.RIGHT, boiler2_pos)
engine2_pos = Position(x=boiler2.position.x + 3, y=boiler2.position.y)
move_to(engine2_pos)
engine2 = place_entity(Prototype.SteamEngine, Direction.RIGHT, engine2_pos)

# Connect water system
pipes1 = connect_entities(pump, boiler1, Prototype.Pipe)
pipes2 = connect_entities(pump, boiler2, Prototype.Pipe)

# Place electric pole between engines to create power network
pole_pos = Position(x=engine1.position.x, y=(engine1.position.y + engine2.position.y) / 2)
move_to(pole_pos)
pole = place_entity(Prototype.SmallElectricPole, Direction.RIGHT, pole_pos)

# Set up coal mining
move_to(coal_position)
drill = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, Direction.RIGHT, coal_position)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, drill, 5)

# Connect miner to boilers with belts
# Create straight belt line from miner to between boilers
belt_segments = []
current_pos = drill.drop_position
target_y = (boiler1.position.y + boiler2.position.y) / 2

while abs(current_pos.y - target_y) > 0.5:
    next_pos = Position(x=current_pos.x, y=current_pos.y + 1)
    move_to(current_pos)
    belt = place_entity(Prototype.TransportBelt, Direction.DOWN, current_pos)
    belt_segments.append(belt)
    current_pos = next_pos

# Create belt split to boilers
move_to(current_pos)
split_belt = place_entity(Prototype.TransportBelt, Direction.LEFT, current_pos)

# Connect to boiler 1
current_pos = split_belt.position
while current_pos.x > boiler1.position.x - 1:
    next_pos = Position(x=current_pos.x - 1, y=boiler1.position.y)
    move_to(current_pos)
    belt = place_entity(Prototype.TransportBelt, Direction.LEFT, current_pos)
    current_pos = next_pos

# Connect to boiler 2
current_pos = split_belt.position
while current_pos.x > boiler2.position.x - 1:
    next_pos = Position(x=current_pos.x - 1, y=boiler2.position.y)
    move_to(current_pos)
    belt = place_entity(Prototype.TransportBelt, Direction.LEFT, current_pos)
    current_pos = next_pos

# Add inserters for boilers
inserter1_pos = Position(x=boiler1.position.x - 1, y=boiler1.position.y)
move_to(inserter1_pos)
inserter1 = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerInserter, Direction.LEFT, inserter1_pos)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, inserter1, 1)

inserter2_pos = Position(x=boiler2.position.x - 1, y=boiler2.position.y)
move_to(inserter2_pos)
inserter2 = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerInserter, Direction.LEFT, inserter2_pos)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, inserter2, 1)

# Initial fuel for boilers
move_to(boiler1.position)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, boiler1, 5)
move_to(boiler2.position)
insert_item(Prototype.Coal, boiler2, 5)

# Monitor system operation
for _ in range(4):
    sleep(30)
    
    # Check power generation
    results = inspect_entities(engine1.position, radius=20)
    engines = results.get_entities(Prototype.SteamEngine)
    boilers = results.get_entities(Prototype.Boiler)
    
    for engine in engines:
        if engine.status == EntityStatus.NOT_PLUGGED_IN_ELECTRIC_NETWORK:
            continue
        assert engine.status == EntityStatus.WORKING, "Steam engine not generating power"
        
    # Check fuel distribution
    for boiler in boilers:
        if boiler.status not in [EntityStatus.WORKING, EntityStatus.FULL_OUTPUT]:
            assert boiler.status == EntityStatus.WORKING or boiler.status == EntityStatus.FULL_OUTPUT, "Boiler not operating correctly"
        fuel = inspect_inventory(boiler).get(Prototype.Coal, 0)
        assert fuel > 0, "Boiler running out of fuel"

print("Power plant setup validated and operational")

copper_furnace = place_entity(Prototype.StoneFurnace, Direction.SOUTH, copper_furnace_pos)
assert copper_furnace, "Failed to place copper furnace"

# Setup turret production
assembler_pos = Position(x=iron_furnace.position.x+4, y=iron_furnace.position.y)
turret_assembler = place_entity(Prototype.AssemblingMachine1, Direction.SOUTH, assembler_pos)
assert turret_assembler, "Failed to place turret assembler"

# Setup ammo production
ammo_assembler_pos = Position(x=turret_assembler.position.x+3, y=turret_assembler.position.y)
ammo_assembler = place_entity(Prototype.AssemblingMachine1, Direction.SOUTH, ammo_assembler_pos)
assert ammo_assembler, "Failed to place ammo assembler"

# Create defensive perimeter
perimeter_points = [
    Position(x=ammo_assembler.position.x+5, y=ammo_assembler.position.y),
    Position(x=ammo_assembler.position.x+5, y=ammo_assembler.position.y+5),
    Position(x=ammo_assembler.position.x+5, y=ammo_assembler.position.y-5)
]

turrets = []
for pos in perimeter_points:
    turret = place_entity(Prototype.GunTurret, Direction.EAST, pos)
    if turret:
        turrets.append(turret)
        # Add belt and inserter for ammo supply
        belt = place_entity(Prototype.TransportBelt, Direction.EAST, 
                          Position(x=pos.x-1, y=pos.y))
        inserter = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerInserter, Direction.EAST,
                              Position(x=pos.x-2, y=pos.y))
        assert belt and inserter, f"Failed to place ammo supply at {pos}"

assert len(turrets) == len(perimeter_points), "Failed to place all turrets"

# Verify final setup
entities = inspect_entities(turret_assembler.position, radius=20)
assert entities.count(Prototype.GunTurret) == len(perimeter_points), "Missing turrets"
assert entities.count(Prototype.TransportBelt) >= len(perimeter_points), "Missing supply belts"
assert entities.count(Prototype.BurnerInserter) >= len(perimeter_points), "Missing inserters"

    # First move to nearest coal to start
    coal_pos = nearest(Resource.Coal)
    move_to(coal_pos)
    
    # Setup coal mining
    coal_patch = get_resource_patch(Resource.Coal, coal_pos)

    # Wait for coal production
    sleep(5)
    harvest_resource(coal_pos, 20)
    insert_item(Prototype.Coal, coal_drill, 5)

    # Move to iron and setup mining/smelting 
    iron_pos = nearest(Resource.IronOre)

[2024-10-28 20:43:52] def setup_defense_perimeter():
    # First move to nearest coal to start
    coal_pos = nearest(Resource.Coal)
    move_to(coal_pos)
    
    # Setup coal mining
    coal_patch = get_resource_patch(Resource.Coal, coal_pos)
    coal_drill = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, Direction.SOUTH, coal_patch.bounding_box.center)
    coal_chest = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.WoodenChest, coal_drill.position, Direction.SOUTH)
    
    # Wait for coal production
    sleep(5)
    harvest_resource(coal_pos, 20)
    insert_item(Prototype.Coal, coal_drill, 5)

    # Move to iron and setup mining/smelting
    iron_pos = nearest(Resource.IronOre) 
    move_to(iron_pos)

    iron_patch = get_resource_patch(Resource.IronOre, iron_pos)
    iron_drill = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, Direction.SOUTH, iron_patch.bounding_box.center)
    iron_furnace = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.StoneFurnace, iron_drill.position, Direction.SOUTH, spacing=1)
    iron_chest = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.WoodenChest, iron_furnace.position, Direction.SOUTH)
    iron_drill_inserter = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter, iron_drill.position, Direction.SOUTH)
    iron_furnace_inserter = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter, iron_furnace.position, Direction.SOUTH)

    # Insert coal into iron production
    for entity in [iron_drill, iron_furnace, iron_drill_inserter, iron_furnace_inserter]:
        insert_item(Prototype.Coal, entity, 5)

    # Wait for iron plate production
    sleep(10)
    harvest_resource(iron_pos, 20)

    # Move to copper and setup mining/smelting
    copper_pos = nearest(Resource.CopperOre)
    move_to(copper_pos)
    
    copper_patch = get_resource_patch(Resource.CopperOre, copper_pos)
    copper_drill = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, Direction.SOUTH, copper_patch.bounding_box.center)
    copper_furnace = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.StoneFurnace, copper_drill.position, Direction.SOUTH, spacing=1)
    copper_chest = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.WoodenChest, copper_furnace.position, Direction.SOUTH)
    copper_drill_inserter = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter, copper_drill.position, Direction.SOUTH)
    copper_furnace_inserter = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter, copper_furnace.position, Direction.SOUTH)

    # Insert coal into copper production
    for entity in [copper_drill, copper_furnace, copper_drill_inserter, copper_furnace_inserter]:
        insert_item(Prototype.Coal, entity, 5)

    # Wait for copper plate production
    sleep(10)
    harvest_resource(copper_pos, 20)

    # Extract produced materials
    extract_item(Prototype.IronPlate, iron_chest.position, 20)
    extract_item(Prototype.CopperPlate, copper_chest.position, 20)

    # Craft intermediate items
    craft_item(Prototype.IronGearWheel, 10)
    craft_item(Prototype.CopperCable, 10) 
    craft_item(Prototype.ElectronicCircuit, 5)

    # Setup assemblers
    assembler_pos = Position(x=iron_furnace.position.x+4, y=iron_furnace.position.y)
    move_to(assembler_pos)
    
    # Craft and place assemblers
    craft_item(Prototype.AssemblingMachine1, 2)
    turret_assembler = place_entity(Prototype.AssemblingMachine1, Direction.SOUTH, assembler_pos)
    ammo_assembler = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.AssemblingMachine1, turret_assembler.position, Direction.EAST, spacing=2)

    # Set assembler recipes
    set_entity_recipe(turret_assembler, Prototype.GunTurret)
    set_entity_recipe(ammo_assembler, Prototype.FirearmMagazine)

    # Insert materials into assemblers
    insert_item(Prototype.IronPlate, turret_assembler, 20)
    insert_item(Prototype.CopperPlate, turret_assembler, 10)
    insert_item(Prototype.IronGearWheel, turret_assembler, 10)
    insert_item(Prototype.IronPlate, ammo_assembler, 20)

    # Wait for production
    sleep(10)

    # Create defensive line
    perimeter_points = [
        Position(x=ammo_assembler.position.x+3, y=ammo_assembler.position.y),
        Position(x=ammo_assembler.position.x+3, y=ammo_assembler.position.y+3),
        Position(x=ammo_assembler.position.x+3, y=ammo_assembler.position.y-3)
    ]

    for pos in perimeter_points:
        move_to(pos)
        craft_item(Prototype.GunTurret, 1)
        craft_item(Prototype.FirearmMagazine, 10)
        turret = place_entity(Prototype.GunTurret, Direction.EAST, pos)
        if turret:
            insert_item(Prototype.FirearmMagazine, turret, 10)
            belt = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.TransportBelt, turret.position, Direction.WEST)
            inserter = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter, belt.position, Direction.WEST)
            insert_item(Prototype.Coal, inserter, 5)

    copper_drill_inserter = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter, copper_drill.position, Direction.SOUTH)
    copper_furnace_inserter = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter, copper_furnace.position, Direction.SOUTH)

    # Insert coal into copper production
    for entity in [copper_drill, copper_furnace, copper_drill_inserter, copper_furnace_inserter]:
        insert_item(Prototype.Coal, entity, 5)

    # Wait for copper plate production
    sleep(10)
    harvest_resource(copper_pos, 20)

    # Extract produced materials
    move_to(iron_chest.position)
    extract_item(Prototype.IronPlate, iron_chest.position, 20)
    move_to(copper_chest.position)
    extract_item(Prototype.CopperPlate, copper_chest.position, 20)

    # Craft intermediate items
    craft_item(Prototype.IronGearWheel, 10)
    craft_item(Prototype.CopperCable, 10)
    craft_item(Prototype.ElectronicCircuit, 5)

    # Setup assemblers
    assembler_pos = Position(x=iron_furnace.position.x+4, y=iron_furnace.position.y) 
    move_to(assembler_pos)
    
    # Craft and place assemblers
    craft_item(Prototype.AssemblingMachine1, 2)
    turret_assembler = place_entity(Prototype.AssemblingMachine1, Direction.SOUTH, assembler_pos)
    move_to(turret_assembler.position)
    ammo_assembler = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.AssemblingMachine1, turret_assembler.position, Direction.EAST, spacing=2)

    # Set assembler recipes
    set_entity_recipe(turret_assembler, Prototype.GunTurret)
    set_entity_recipe(ammo_assembler, Prototype.FirearmMagazine)

    # Insert materials into assemblers
    insert_item(Prototype.IronPlate, turret_assembler, 20)
    insert_item(Prototype.CopperPlate, turret_assembler, 10)
    insert_item(Prototype.IronGearWheel, turret_assembler, 10)
    insert_item(Prototype.IronPlate, ammo_assembler, 20)

    # Wait for production
    sleep(10)

    # Create defensive line
    perimeter_points = [
        Position(x=ammo_assembler.position.x+3, y=ammo_assembler.position.y),
        Position(x=ammo_assembler.position.x+3, y=ammo_assembler.position.y+3),
        Position(x=ammo_assembler.position.x+3, y=ammo_assembler.position.y-3)
    ]

    for pos in perimeter_points:
        move_to(pos)
        craft_item(Prototype.GunTurret, 1)
        craft_item(Prototype.FirearmMagazine, 10)
        turret = place_entity(Prototype.GunTurret, Direction.EAST, pos)
        if turret:
            insert_item(Prototype.FirearmMagazine, turret, 10)
            belt = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.TransportBelt, turret.position, Direction.WEST)
            move_to(belt.position)
            inserter = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter, belt.position, Direction.WEST)
            insert_item(Prototype.Coal, inserter, 5)

    insert_item(Prototype.IronGearWheel, turret_assembler, 10)
    insert_item(Prototype.IronPlate, ammo_assembler, 20)

    sleep(15)

    # Create defensive positions
    radius = 8
    center = ammo_assembler.position
    perimeter_points = [
        Position(x=center.x+radius, y=center.y),
        Position(x=center.x+radius, y=center.y+radius),
        Position(x=center.x+radius, y=center.y-radius),
        Position(x=center.x, y=center.y+radius),
        Position(x=center.x, y=center.y-radius)
    ]

    for pos in perimeter_points:
        move_to(pos)
        turret = place_entity(Prototype.GunTurret, Direction.EAST, pos)
        if turret:
            insert_item(Prototype.FirearmMagazine, turret, 10)
            belt = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.TransportBelt, turret.position, Direction.WEST)
            inserter = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter, belt.position, Direction.EAST)
            insert_item(Prototype.Coal, inserter, 5)
            move_to(inserter.position)

[2024-10-28 20:46:57] def setup_defense_perimeter():
    # First move to nearest coal to start
    coal_pos = nearest(Resource.Coal)
    move_to(coal_pos)
    
    # Setup coal mining
    coal_patch = get_resource_patch(Resource.Coal, coal_pos)
    coal_drill = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, Direction.SOUTH, coal_patch.bounding_box.center)
    coal_chest = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.WoodenChest, coal_drill.position, Direction.SOUTH)
    
    # Harvest initial coal manually
    harvest_resource(coal_pos, 50)
    insert_item(Prototype.Coal, coal_drill, 5)

    # Move to iron and setup mining/smelting
    iron_pos = nearest(Resource.IronOre) 
    move_to(iron_pos)

    iron_patch = get_resource_patch(Resource.IronOre, iron_pos)
    iron_drill = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, Direction.SOUTH, iron_patch.bounding_box.center)
    
    # Setup iron smelting line
    iron_furnace = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.StoneFurnace, iron_drill.position, Direction.SOUTH, spacing=1)
    iron_chest = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.WoodenChest, iron_furnace.position, Direction.SOUTH)
    iron_drill_inserter = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter, iron_drill.position, Direction.SOUTH)
    iron_furnace_inserter = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter, iron_furnace.position, Direction.SOUTH)

    # Power iron production line
    for entity in [iron_drill, iron_drill_inserter, iron_furnace, iron_furnace_inserter]:
        insert_item(Prototype.Coal, entity, 5)
    
    # Manually harvest initial iron
    harvest_resource(iron_pos, 20)
    sleep(10)

    # Setup copper production
    copper_pos = nearest(Resource.CopperOre)
    move_to(copper_pos)

    copper_patch = get_resource_patch(Resource.CopperOre, copper_pos)
    copper_drill = place_entity(Prototype.BurnerMiningDrill, Direction.SOUTH, copper_patch.bounding_box.center)
    
    # Setup copper smelting line
    copper_furnace = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.StoneFurnace, copper_drill.position, Direction.SOUTH, spacing=1)
    copper_chest = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.WoodenChest, copper_furnace.position, Direction.SOUTH)
    copper_drill_inserter = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter, copper_drill.position, Direction.SOUTH)
    copper_furnace_inserter = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.BurnerInserter, copper_furnace.position, Direction.SOUTH)

    # Power copper production line
    for entity in [copper_drill, copper_drill_inserter, copper_furnace, copper_furnace_inserter]:
        insert_item(Prototype.Coal, entity, 5)

    # Manually harvest initial copper
    harvest_resource(copper_pos, 20)
    sleep(10)

    # Collect materials
    move_to(iron_chest.position)
    extract_item(Prototype.IronPlate, iron_chest.position, 20)
    move_to(copper_chest.position) 
    extract_item(Prototype.CopperPlate, copper_chest.position, 20)

    # Craft intermediate items
    craft_item(Prototype.IronGearWheel, 20)
    craft_item(Prototype.CopperCable, 20) 
    craft_item(Prototype.ElectronicCircuit, 10)

    # Setup assembling machines
    assembler_pos = Position(x=iron_furnace.position.x+5, y=iron_furnace.position.y)
    move_to(assembler_pos)

    craft_item(Prototype.AssemblingMachine1, 2)
    turret_assembler = place_entity(Prototype.AssemblingMachine1, Direction.SOUTH, assembler_pos)
    ammo_assembler = place_entity_next_to(Prototype.AssemblingMachine1, turret_assembler.position, Direction.EAST, spacing=2)

    # Configure assemblers
    set_entity_recipe(turret_assembler, Prototype.GunTurret)
    set_entity_recipe(ammo_assembler, Prototype.FirearmMagazine)

    # Feed materials
    insert_item(Prototype.IronPlate, turret_assembler, 20)
    insert_item(Prototype.CopperPlate, turret_assembler, 10)
    insert_item(Prototype.IronGearWheel, turret_assembler, 10)
    insert_item(Prototype.IronPlate, ammo_assembler, 20)

    sleep(15)

    # Create defensive positions

    center = ammo_assembler.position

        Position(x=center.x+radius, y=center.y),
        Position(x=center.x+radius, y=center.y+radius),
        Position(x=center.x+radius, y=center.y-radius),
        Position(x=center.x, y=center.y+radius),
        Position(x=center.x, y=center.y-radius)
    ]

    for pos in perimeter_points:
        move_to(pos)
        if can_place_entity(Prototype.GunTurret, Direction.EAST, pos):
            turret = place_entity(Prototype.GunTurret, Direction.EAST, pos)
            insert_item(Prototype.FirearmMagazine, turret, 10)
